1px;\">还有网友表示，自己认为代言一款手游是很不体面的事情，中国的95%以上的手游就是骗钱，而不是花钱购买好的艺术体验感，罗老师这波实在不是体面的代言，所有人都看出你是在还债。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">对此，罗永浩回应称，跟还债无必然关系。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><img margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\"rich_pages aligncenter\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; width: 677px !important; visibility: visible !important;\" title=\"罗永浩代言手游了！变身“渣渣浩”，终于活成他讨厌的样子？\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/5-1598447720.jpeg\" alt=\"罗永浩代言手游了！变身“渣渣浩”，终于活成他讨厌的样子？\" /></p>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">老罗是个理想主义者，网友质疑他代言手游是践踏了理想主义：“你们怎么知道他是还债？打着还债口号践踏理想主义，实际上是自己赚钱吧。”</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">对此，罗永浩回复称，还不还债自己都可以代言游戏。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\"rich_pages aligncenter\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; width: 567px !important; visibility: visible !important;\" title=\"罗永浩代言手游了！变身“渣渣浩”，终于活成他讨厌的样子？\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/4-1598447720.jpeg\" alt=\"罗永浩代言手游了！变身“渣渣浩”，终于活成他讨厌的样子？\" /></p>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">有些人认为凭自己本事挣钱有啥问题吗？什么时候赚钱都变成了错的事；理想主义和赚钱有冲突？代言手游见不得人，虽然广告确实low了点。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\"rich_pages aligncenter\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; width: 677px !important; visibility: visible !important;\" title=\"罗永浩代言手游了！变身“渣渣浩”，终于活成他讨厌的样子？\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/8-1598447721.jpeg\" alt=\"罗永浩代言手游了！变身“渣渣浩”，终于活成他讨厌的样子？\" /></p>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">也有人支持老罗，认为他活得明白。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\"rich_pages aligncenter\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; width: 677px !important; visibility: visible !important;\" title=\"罗永浩代言手游了！变身“渣渣浩”，终于活成他讨厌的样子？\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/9-1598447722.jpeg\" alt=\"罗永浩代言手游了！变身“渣渣浩”，终于活成他讨厌的样子？\" /></p>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">但网友觉得罗永浩活成了他自己最讨厌的样子，罗永浩反驳称，怎么会，自己讨厌的其实是你这种傻子。</span></p>\n<h2 style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600; font-size: 18px;\"><strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">游戏广告简单粗暴、被指low</span></strong></span></h2>\n<h2 style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600; font-size: 18px;\"><strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">大半个娱乐圈都代言了</span></strong></span></h2>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">其实名人代言手游一直不被部分网友接受。部分原因是因为手游的广告大范围刷屏、广告海报简单粗暴、游戏玩法创意千篇一律，制作简陋，引起视觉疲劳等。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">特别是游戏海报和广告语，很多都是举着大刀、喊着是兄弟就来啃我。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">因此代言这类手游被网友认为low、掉价，可尽管如此，仍有很多明星去代言这类游戏。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\"rich_pages aligncenter\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; visibility: visible !important; width: 645px !important;\" title=\"罗永浩代言手游了！变身“渣渣浩”，终于活成他讨厌的样子？\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/4-1598447722.jpeg\" alt=\"罗永浩代言手游了！变身“渣渣浩”，终于活成他讨厌的样子？\" /></p>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\"rich_pages aligncenter\" style=\"text-align: center; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; visibility: visible !important; width: 645px !important;\" title=\"罗永浩代言手游了！变身“渣渣浩”，终于活成他讨厌的样子？\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/7-1598447722.jpeg\" alt=\"罗永浩代言手游了！变身“渣渣浩”，终于活成他讨厌的样子？\" /></p>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\"rich_pages aligncenter\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; visibility: visible !important; width: 645px !important;\" title=\"罗永浩代言手游了！变身“渣渣浩”，终于活成他讨厌的样子？\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/9-1598447722-1.jpeg\" alt=\"罗永浩代言手游了！变身“渣渣浩”，终于活成他讨厌的样子？\" /></p>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\"js_darkmode__0 aligncenter\" style=\"color: #000000; text-align: start; font-size: 15px; caret-color: #000000; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; visibility: visible !important; width: 541.648px !important;\" title=\"罗永浩代言手游了！变身“渣渣浩”，终于活成他讨厌的样子？\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/7-1598447723.jpeg\" alt=\"罗永浩代言手游了！变身“渣渣浩”，终于活成他讨厌的样子？\" /></p>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\"rich_pages aligncenter\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; visibility: visible !important; width: 645px !important;\" title=\"罗永浩代言手游了！变身“渣渣浩”，终于活成他讨厌的样子？\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/3-1598447723.jpeg\" alt=\"罗永浩代言手游了！变身“渣渣浩”，终于活成他讨厌的样子？\" /></p>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\"rich_pages aligncenter\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; visibility: visible !important; width: 645px !important;\" title=\"罗永浩代言手游了！变身“渣渣浩”，终于活成他讨厌的样子？\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/4-1598447723.jpeg\" alt=\"罗永浩代言手游了！变身“渣渣浩”，终于活成他讨厌的样子？\" /></p>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\"js_darkmode__1 aligncenter\" style=\"color: #000000; caret-color: #000000; font-family: -webkit-standard; text-align: start; top: 48px; left: 203px; cursor: pointer; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; visibility: visible !important; width: 645px !important;\" title=\"罗永浩代言手游了！变身“渣渣浩”，终于活成他讨厌的样子？\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/9-1598447723.jpeg\" alt=\"罗永浩代言手游了！变身“渣渣浩”，终于活成他讨厌的样子？\" width=\"390.10989010989\" height=\"355\" /></p>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\"rich_pages aligncenter\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; visibility: visible !important; width: 599px !important;\" title=\"罗永浩代言手游了！变身“渣渣浩”，终于活成他讨厌的样子？\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/4-1598447724.jpeg\" alt=\"罗永浩代言手游了！变身“渣渣浩”，终于活成他讨厌的样子？\" /></p>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\"rich_pages aligncenter\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; visibility: visible !important; width: 645px !important;\" title=\"罗永浩代言手游了！变身“渣渣浩”，终于活成他讨厌的样子？\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/0-1598447724.jpeg\" alt=\"罗永浩代言手游了！变身“渣渣浩”，终于活成他讨厌的样子？\" /></p>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\"rich_pages aligncenter\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; visibility: visible !important; width: 645px !important;\" title=\"罗永浩代言手游了！变身“渣渣浩”，终于活成他讨厌的样子？\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/2-1598447724.jpeg\" alt=\"罗永浩代言手游了！变身“渣渣浩”，终于活成他讨厌的样子？\" /></p>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">李连杰、成龙、古天乐、黎明、甄子丹、郭富城、张家辉、陈小春、胡军、孙红雷、吴孟达、张卫健、宋小宝、王宝强、刘烨、邓超、曾志伟、林子聪、樊少皇、岳云鹏、吴镇宇、黄子韬、张子健、吴志雄、迪丽热巴等等诸多明星都曾代言过各种网页游戏、手机游戏。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">而明星之所以去代言此类游戏，丰厚的代言费用是重要原因。据网络爆料，张家辉首次合作代言费为500万一年，而选择继续续约的古天乐代言费涨到了1000万。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">此类游戏收入也十分可观，游戏《贪玩蓝月》在张家辉代言时期仅3个月内获得了49万下载量，186万美元收入。《一刀传世》在9个月的时间内获得了425万下载量，超过6300万美元的收入。《大唐无双莽战传》则在三年内获得了近150万下载量，近3200万美元收入。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">有业内人士称，上述只是iOS平台收入，安卓平台的收入可能更多。</span></p>\n<h2 style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600; font-size: 18px;\"><strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">罗永浩活成他最讨厌的样子？</span></strong></span></h2>\n<h2 style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600; font-size: 18px;\"><strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">为了还钱曾做过“low产品”</span></strong></span></h2>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">其实，代言手游并非罗永浩第一次被质疑不体面，早在罗永浩宣布直播带货的时候，就有无数质疑的声音响起。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">“老罗偶像崩塌，跌落神坛，太让人失望了，为了赚钱去做卑微的主播。”</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\"rich_pages aligncenter\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; width: 640px !important; visibility: visible !important;\" title=\"罗永浩代言手游了！变身“渣渣浩”，终于活成他讨厌的样子？\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/2-1598447724-1.jpeg\" alt=\"罗永浩代言手游了！变身“渣渣浩”，终于活成他讨厌的样子？\" /></p>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">但罗永浩回复：失望？怎么会，我在想各种办法赚钱还债啊，做主播赚的又不是脏钱。我对自己很佩服，不想还好，一想就肃然起敬想求签名那种。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\"rich_pages aligncenter\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; width: 640px !important; visibility: visible !important;\" title=\"罗永浩代言手游了！变身“渣渣浩”，终于活成他讨厌的样子？\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/5-1598447725.jpeg\" alt=\"罗永浩代言手游了！变身“渣渣浩”，终于活成他讨厌的样子？\" /></p>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">而对于活成自己年轻时最讨厌的样子，罗永浩此前回应称，“如果非要谈谈我现在讨厌自己什么，那就是因为工作职责的关系，我不能想说什么就说什么，不能直接干这些笨蛋的XX了。”</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">对于代言手游，老罗自己并不认为low，但罗永浩曾公开承认自己为了还钱做过很low的产品。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">在“老人与海”黑科技发布会上，他表示，当初为急于还债权方的钱，也做了很low的叫聊天宝的东西，赶紧还了钱才是最不low的事。但是Low完了也没有成功。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 8px; margin-left: 8px; white-space: normal; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">看来，老罗为了还债费劲了心思，那么对于老罗代言手游你怎么看？</span></p>\n</div>\n<p>&#160;</p>\n<p>&#160;</p>\n<section> #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">ｃ、介绍话术：添加成功之后，第一句发什么，后面发什么，什么话术结尾？</span><span style=\"color: #3f3f3f; font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">要不要对被祝福者做转化，这些都是需要注意的地方。</span></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">目的就是为了强调，吸引被祝福者的注意，以及激发被祝福者想要购买和了解的欲望，这些都是要设计的环节。</span></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"></section>\n<section 1px;\">2.找准渠道截流</span></strong></span></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; 1px;\">想告诉大家的是，一个活动一定是用户参与门槛很低，用户广，而不是只针对一小部分人的活动。</span></strong></span></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">还有就是要让参与双方都能从中有参与感＼收获感，这份收货可能是惊喜＼冲突＼美好等等。</span></strong></span></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">３.如何再次抓住机会</span></strong></span></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">除了我们刚才提到的爆款公式外，各位可以把一年中的重大节日做个罗列。</span></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">比如情人节＼七夕＼中秋＼圣诞＼等有代表性，又可以有创意性的节日，大家就可以提前筹备起来。</span></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">大家想想，这次是添加好友发短信。</span></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">难道不能变通一下，变成打电话说祝福呢？能不能变成上门呢？能不能变成寄快递呢？</span></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">还有大家想想这几年特别火爆的非洲小孩说祝福的话，那可不可把非洲换成其他州＼其他民族或者改成唱歌、跳舞呢？</span></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">而且还是刚才提到的案例，当大家都在关注七夕蛤蟆的时候，有的人就做了七夕布谷鸟（不孤独、不哭），也依然有许多人下单购买。</span></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">所以很多时候，只要稍微变通一下就行。</span></strong></span></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">４.有需求就有市场</span></strong></span></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">除了七夕蛤蟆祝福的服务，各位完全可以把思路开阔一下。</span></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">一种是赚懒人的服务，一种是赚技能服务，还有一种是赚猎奇的服务，也包括赚面子的服务。</span></strong></span></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">淘宝上有一个叫醒服务，已经存在好多年了。</span></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">我看到其中一个商家提供的叫醒服务，当月销售１８７９份，店铺评分全部４.９飘红。</span></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">不仅提供一个月的，还可以包年＼包季度的。</span></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">那么提供叫醒服务可以做，能不能提供提醒服务呢？</span></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em; text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages 1px;\">再如不久前的老照片修复＼生成卡通照这些赚钱小项目，本质就是利用信息差和技能，赚取用户的钱。</span></strong></span></section>\n<section style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"></section>\n<section
